Abstract: This paper presents an experimental study of motion planning for resilient continuum robots. In this study we mainly focused on multi-criteria decision-making, its application for path-planning algorithms, impact on the generated path and execution time. To do this, we used two well-known algorithms for path planning, namely Genetic algorithm and A star algorithm, and modified them by adding the Analytical Hierarchy Process algorithm to evaluate the quality of the paths generated. In our experiment the Analytical Hierarchy Process considers four different criteria, i.e. distance, motors damage, mechanical damage of the robot's arm and accuracy, each considered to contribute to the resilience of a continuum robot. The use of different criteria is necessary to increase the time to maintenance operations of the continuum robot. We conducted the experiments using two different simulated environments of the robot. Although we significantly simplified the robot's model and its environment, we still implemented some of the features of the environment based on the real robot prototype. In particular, one of the environments has single- as well as multi-path points, and other consists of the multi-path points only. The results show that, in contrast to A star, the performance time of Genetic algorithm does not depend on the environment's cardinality. It generates more diverse paths, which increases the robot's resilience.

</details>


### [235] [Generating Robot Hands from Human Demonstrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20549)
*Sha Yi,Nicklas Hansen,Xueqian Bai,Carmelo Sferrazza,Michael T. Tolley,Xiaolong Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一个数据驱动的框架，利用人类演示数据生成机器人手部设计，通过匹配人类指尖运动轨迹来优化机械结构，使用强化学习加速搜索过程，并成功制造出性能优于商业产品的6自由度通用手和3自由度任务专用手。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人学习在控制方面进展迅速，但机器人身体设计的学习仍然困难，因为同时搜索设计和控制会形成巨大的组合问题。需要一种方法能够利用人类演示数据来优化机器人物理结构。

Method: 1. 使用超过400万帧人类指尖日常操作运动数据作为参考
2. 采用简单的控制策略：通过逆运动学匹配人类指尖位置
3. 优化树状结构的机器人手设计以复现目标运动
4. 训练强化学习智能体提出好的手部设计和关节角度，将搜索时间从数小时减少到数分钟
5. 使用一体式3D打印结构制造，包含打印即用的关节

Result: 1. 生成了6自由度通用机器人手，在遥操作指尖跟踪方面比现有商业机器人手更准确
2. 生成了3自由度任务专用手，能够以更低的机械复杂度复现结构化的人类和合成轨迹
3. 实现了从数小时到数分钟的搜索时间优化

Conclusion: 大规模人类运动数据不仅可以用于训练机器人控制器，还可以作为优化和生成机器人物理实体的参考，为机器人身体设计提供了新的数据驱动方法。

Abstract: Robot learning has advanced rapidly in learning control, but learning the physical body of a robot remains much more difficult because jointly searching over design and control creates a very large combinatorial problem. Here, we present a data-driven framework for generating robot hands from human demonstrations. Instead of learning a complex controller together with each candidate design, we generate robot hand designs using the same simple control policy used after fabrication: matching fingertip positions through inverse kinematics. Using more than 4 million frames of human fingertip motion from everyday manipulation, our algorithm optimizes tree-structured robot hands to reproduce desired target motions. The framework produced both a 6-degree-of-freedom (DoF) general-purpose hand and lower-DoF task-specific hands with spatial four-bar mimic joints. To accelerate the search over designs, we trained a reinforcement-learning (RL) actor to propose good hand designs and joint angles, reducing search time from hours to minutes. We fabricated the mechanisms directly as one-piece articulated structures with print-in-place joints. In real-world experiments, the 6-DoF hand achieved highly accurate teleoperated fingertip tracking better than available commercial robot hands, whereas the specialized 3-DoF hands reproduced structured human and synthetic trajectories with reduced mechanical complexity. These results showed that large-scale human motion data can be used not only to train robot controllers but also as a reference for optimizing and generating the physical embodiment of robots.

### [236] [MemoryWAM: Efficient World Action Modeling with Persistent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20562)
*Sizhe Yang,Juncheng Mu,Tianming Wei,Chenhao Lu,Xiaofan Li,Linning Xu,Zhengrong Xue,Zhecheng Yuan,Dahua Lin,Jiangmiao Pang,Huazhe Xu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: MemoryWAM：一种具有高效持久记忆的世界动作模型，通过混合记忆设计解决现有WAM在非马尔可夫环境中的效率-历史长度权衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界动作模型面临基本权衡：高效推理方法通常只基于有限观察窗口，在非马尔可夫环境中表现不佳；而保留长历史的方法则随序列长度显著增加时间和空间成本。需要一种既能保持长历史记忆又具有高效推理能力的模型。

Method: MemoryWAM采用混合记忆设计，结合近期帧、事件边界锚帧和压缩的gist标记来总结长程历史。通过定制的注意力机制实现详细短期上下文和压缩长期上下文的检索。

Result: 在仿真和真实世界的长时程、依赖记忆的操纵任务中，MemoryWAM优于强大的视觉-语言-动作模型和WAM基线，同时保持了良好的计算效率。

Conclusion: MemoryWAM通过高效持久记忆设计成功解决了WAM在非马尔可夫环境中的效率-历史长度权衡问题，为机器人操纵提供了一种既强大又高效的世界模型解决方案。

Abstract: Robust robotic manipulation in the real world requires not only an understanding of the current observation, but also memory and dynamics modeling. World action models (WAMs) possess these capabilities by jointly modeling visual foresight and actions conditioned on both current and historical observations, making them a promising paradigm for robotic manipulation. However, existing WAMs face a fundamental trade-off: methods with efficient inference typically condition only on a bounded window of recent observations and therefore struggle in non-Markovian environments, whereas methods that preserve long histories incur time and space costs that grow substantially with sequence length. To address this challenge, we introduce MemoryWAM, a world action model with efficient persistent memory. MemoryWAM uses a hybrid memory design that combines recent frames, event-boundary anchor frames, and compact gist tokens that summarize long-range history. A tailored attention mechanism enables retrieval of both detailed short-term context and compressed long-term context, supporting memory-dependent decision-making with reduced inference latency and GPU memory usage. Across long-horizon, memory-dependent manipulation tasks in both simulation and the real world, MemoryWAM outperforms strong vision-language-action (VLA) and WAM baselines while maintaining favorable computational efficiency.

### [237] [Human Universal Grasping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17054)
*Kevin Yuanbo Wu,Tianxing Zhou,Isaac Tu,Billy Yan,Irmak Guzey,David Fouhey,Dandan Shan,Lerrel Pinto*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: HUG是一个基于流匹配的模型，能够从单张RGB-D图像生成多样化的人类抓握姿态，并可通过重定向应用于机器人抓取，在真实世界场景中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类抓握物体轻松自如，而多指机器人远未达到这种通用性。人类每天抓取数千物体，这是最自然的机器人抓取数据来源。

Method: 1. 使用智能眼镜收集1M-HUGs数据集，包含100万帧人类抓握数据；2. 提出基于流匹配的模型，融合RGB和深度信息，输出手腕位置、旋转和MANO手部姿态参数；3. 预测的抓握姿态可重定向到不同机器人手上。

Result: 1. 创建HUG-Bench基准测试，包含90个未见物体的5个几何类别；2. HUG在真实世界30物体测试集上，比现有最优方法提升23%和34%；3. 发布了代码、数据、基准测试、检查点和交互演示。

Conclusion: HUG通过从人类抓取数据中学习，实现了零样本的机器人抓取能力，在多样化的日常场景中表现出色，为机器人抓取研究提供了新的数据和基准。

Abstract: Humans can grasp objects effortlessly, whereas multi-fingered robots are far from this level of generality. We argue that the most natural source of robot grasping data is from humans, who pick up thousands of objects every day. We present HUG, a flow-matching model that generates diverse human grasps for any user-specified object in a single RGB-D image captured from a stereo camera. Using smart glasses, we first collect 1M-HUGs, an egocentric dataset of human grasps spanning 1M frames (27.8 hrs) and 6,707 object instances across 41 buildings. Next, to model the distribution of natural human grasps, our novel flow-matching model fuses RGB and depth observations to output a grasp parameterized by wrist translation, wrist rotation, and MANO hand pose. Predicted grasps can be retargeted to various robot hands, enabling zero-shot grasping in everyday scenes. To standardize evaluation, we build a new simulated benchmark, HUG-Bench, of 90 unseen objects from five geometric categories and various sizes, with metric-scale 3D meshes. We evaluate HUG in the real world on the 30-object test set of HUG-Bench across multiple stereo cameras, robot embodiments, and household environments. HUG outperforms the state-of-the-art grasping baselines by +23% and +34% on our challenging object set. Code, data, benchmark, checkpoints, and an interactive demo are released on our website: https://grasping.io/

</details>


### [238] [World Engine: Towards the Era of Post-Training for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19836)
*Tianyu Li,Li Chen,Caojun Wang,Haochen Liu,Kashyap Chitta,Zhenjie Yang,Yuhang Lu,Naisheng Ye,Yihang Qiu,Yufei Wang,Luoxi Zou,Jiaxin Peng,Jin Pan,Zhaoyu Su,Andrei Bursuc,Shengbo Eben Li,Andreas Geiger,Peng Su,Hongyang Li*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: World Engine框架通过从真实驾驶日志重建高保真交互环境并系统性地生成安全关键场景变体，用于强化学习后训练，显著提升自动驾驶模型在长尾安全事件中的性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代端到端驾驶策略虽然在常规场景表现优秀，但由于真实驾驶数据集中安全关键的长尾事件稀缺，其可靠性受到限制。这些罕见事件定义了学习策略的实际安全边界，但在现实世界中难以大规模收集。

Method: 引入World Engine生成框架：1）从真实世界日志重建高保真交互环境；2）系统性外推生成现实的安全关键场景变体；3）使用强化学习后训练将策略与安全约束对齐，避免真实世界探索的物理风险。

Result: 在基于nuPlan的公共基准测试中，World Engine显著减少了罕见安全关键场景中的失败，其性能提升远超过仅增加预训练数据。部署到生产级自动驾驶系统后，该策略减少了模拟碰撞，并在实际道路测试中显示出可测量的改进。

Conclusion: 基于合成的安全关键交互进行后训练，为更安全的自动驾驶提供了一条可扩展且有效的途径。完整的代码库套件（包括训练）已向公众发布。

Abstract: Autonomous vehicles must operate safely in the real world, where errors can have severe consequences. Although modern end-to-end driving policies excel in routine scenarios, their reliability is limited by the scarcity of safety-critical ``long-tail'' events in real driving datasets. These rare interactions define the practical safety boundary of the learned policy, yet they are difficult to collect at scale in the real world. Here we show that this fundamental limitation can be addressed by post-training pre-trained driving models on synthesized high-stakes interactions. We introduce World Engine, a generative framework that reconstructs high-fidelity interactive environments from real-world logs and systematically extrapolates them into realistic safety-critical variations. This paradigm enables reinforcement-based post-training to align policies with safety constraints, circumventing the physical risks inherent in real-world exploration. On a public benchmark built on nuPlan, World Engine substantially reduces failures in rare safety-critical scenarios and yields significantly larger gains than scaling pre-training data alone. Furthermore, when deployed on a production-scale autonomous driving system, the resulting policy reduces simulated collisions and demonstrates measurable improvements in on-road testing, showing that post-training on synthesized, safety-critical interactions offers a scalable and effective pathway to safer autonomous driving. The full codebase suite, including training, is released to the public.

</details>


### [239] [MMD-SLAM: Structure-Enhanced Multi-Meta Gaussian Distribution-Guided Visual SLAM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19874)
*Fan Zhu,Ziyu Chen,Peichen Liu,Yifan Zhao,Zhisong Xu,Hui Zhu,Hongxing Zhou,Sixun Liu,Chunmao Jiang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: MMD-SLAM：一种基于亚特兰大世界假设的结构增强视觉SLAM框架，通过点线融合、多Meta高斯表示和Gaussian进化策略，在跟踪精度和建图质量上达到SOTA性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的3DGS-based视觉SLAM方法未能充分利用底层结构信息，限制了渲染质量并导致地图不一致，需要改进结构信息利用以提升性能

Method: 1. 点线融合姿态优化策略，结合3D线段提升跟踪鲁棒性；2. 具有主导方向的多Meta高斯表示，显式编码亚特兰大世界假设的结构先验；3. 适应场景几何的Gaussian进化策略，将结构线索融入全局优化

Conclusion: 通过整合亚特兰大世界假设的结构先验，MMD-SLAM显著提升了3DGS-based视觉SLAM的性能，证明了结构信息在提升SLAM系统鲁棒性和建图质量中的重要性

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has significantly boosted novel view synthesis and high-fidelity scene reconstruction, expanding the potential of 3DGS-based Visual Simultaneous Localization and Mapping (SLAM) methods. However, most existing systems fail to fully exploit the underlying structural information, which limits rendering quality and often leads to inconsistent maps. To address these limitations, we propose MMD-SLAM, a structure-enhanced Visual SLAM framework that leverages the Atlanta World (AW) assumption to guide a Multi-Meta Gaussian representation for photorealistic mapping. First, we introduce a point-line fusion strategy for pose optimization, where 3D line segments are incorporated to improve tracking robustness and provide additional constraints for mapping. Second, we design a Multi-Meta Gaussian representation with dominant directions, explicitly encoding structural priors from the AW hypothesis. Finally, we propose a Gaussian evolution strategy that adapts to scene geometry and incorporates structural cues into global optimization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that these innovations enable MMD-SLAM to achieve state-of-the-art performance in both tracking accuracy and mapping quality. e.g., our method achieves a 48.56% reduction in ATE RMSE on ScanNet and a 5.71% improvement in PSNR on Replica, compared with MonoGS.

### [241] [Deep-Unfolded Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19920)
*Hunter Kuperman,Minchan Jung,Rahul V. Ghosh,Alex Oshin,Evangelos A. Theodorou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Deep Coordinator是一个深度展开框架，通过神经网络动态调整ADMM-DDP分布式优化器的超参数，显著提升多机器人系统轨迹规划效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式优化方法在多机器人系统中虽然可扩展性强，但通常需要针对特定问题进行繁琐的超参数调优，限制了其实际应用效率。

Method: 将固定次数的ADMM-DDP迭代展开为神经网络，在层间加入可学习函数，将优化器状态映射到下一组超参数，并采用无监督学习方案避免监督方法产生的退化解。

Result: 在汽车和四旋翼机群仿真中，Deep Coordinator生成同等质量轨迹的速度比传统求解器快6.18-9.44倍，且在训练规模8倍大的系统中仍保持性能优势。

Conclusion: Deep Coordinator是首个能在求解时动态调整非凸优化器惩罚参数的深度展开框架，显著提升了分布式优化器的效率和可扩展性。

Abstract: Distributed optimization is a highly scalable and structurally transparent technique to solve multi-agent robotics problems; however, such methods often suffer from the need for highly-specialized, problem-specific hyperparameter tunings. In this work, we propose Deep Coordinator, a deep-unfolding framework that learns to dynamically adjust the hyperparameters of ADMM-DDP, a popular distributed solver for robotics tasks, at solve-time in response to optimizer performance. Our architecture consists of unrolling a fixed number of ADMM-DDP iterations into a neural network with learnable functions between layers mapping the optimizer state to the next hyperparameters. To the best of our knowledge, Deep Coordinator is the first deep-unfolding framework to adapt the penalty parameters of a non-convex optimizer at solve-time; we show that the mainstream supervised approach can yield degenerate solutions when training such models, and propose an unsupervised learning scheme. On simulations with fleets of cars and quadrotors, Deep Coordinator produces trajectories of comparable quality 6.18-9.44x faster than conventional solvers. Furthermore, Deep Coordinator retains its performance benefits when deployed to systems up to 8x larger than trained on.

</details>
